Just steps from the sand! Get ready to feel the fresh ocean breeze, listen to the sound of breaking waves and sink your toes into the inviting sand... This ocean front bright and airy 1 bedroom/1 bathroom apartment is a treasure! One could describe the decor as modern simplicity - this apartment is complete with a full-sized bed in the loft, sofa bed in the living area, dining area facing the ocean, kitchen, bathroom and light hardwood floors throughout. After a day on the beach, the living room is the perfect place to relax and unwind. The views are mesmerizing! The apartment is fully furnished and well-equipped. Situated on the boardwalk, this apartment is located in a very walkable neighborhood! Conveniently located to the Santa Monica Pier, Venice, Malibu, Pacific Palisades and Marina Del Rey.
